Go to Starman Source Code Page

This page has the listing of the source code of the Starman interface file.

There is one interface file (*.ifl) for each program. There is also an interface file for the monolith program starman_mon . As the monolith interface file contains all the other interface files, just it is given here. 



#
#   STARMAN_MON.IFL
#
monolith STARMAN_MON
#
#
#      ADDSTARS.IFL
#
interface ADDSTARS
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A ADDSTARS PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.in
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.IN
      position 1
      helpkey 'IN'
      prompt 'Input image to add stars to? (return for none)'
   endparameter
   parameter INSTARS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.instars
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.INSTARS
      position 2
      helpkey 'INSTARS'
      prompt  'Table of input star positions'
   endparameter
   parameter PROFILE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.profile
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.PROFILE
      position 3
      helpkey 'PROFILE'
      prompt  'Profile of stars to add (image)'
   endparameter
   parameter ADD
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.add
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 4
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.ADD
      helpkey 'ADD'
      prompt  'Put stars as +ve or -ve? (add:subtract)'
   endparameter
   parameter OUT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.out
      type    NDF
      access  UPDATE
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.OUT
      position 5
      helpkey 'OUT'
      prompt 'Output image'
   endparameter
   parameter TITLE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.title
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 6
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.TITLE
      helpkey 'TITLE'
      prompt 'Title to add to output image'
   endparameter
   parameter OUTTYPE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.outtype
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 7
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.OUTTYPE
      helpkey 'OUTTYPE'
      prompt '32-bit real/16-bit integer output? (real:short)'
   endparameter
   parameter SIZE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.size
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 8
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.SIZE
      helpkey 'SIZE'
      prompt 'X,Y size of output image'
   endparameter
   parameter DOMAP
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.domap
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 9
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.DOMAP
      helpkey 'DOMAP'
      prompt  'Use empirical map of the profile? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter PYES
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.pyes
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'PYES'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.PYES
      prompt  'Input profile overrides any table profile? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter STARPOIS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.starpois
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'STARPOIS'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.STARPOIS
      prompt  'Add extra Poisson noise for stars? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter STARGAIN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.stargain
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'STARGAIN'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.STARGAIN
      prompt  '((Poisson equivalent)/(star input)) multiplier'
   endparameter
   parameter SEED
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.seed
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SEED'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.SEED
      prompt  'Seed for random number generator'
   endparameter
   parameter SKY
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.sky
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SKY'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.SKY
      prompt  'Sky level to add to image'
   endparameter
   parameter SKYPOIS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.skypois
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SKYPOIS'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.SKYPOIS
      prompt  'Add extra Poisson noise for sky? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter SKYGAIN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.skygain
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SKYGAIN'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.SKYGAIN
      prompt  '((Poisson equivalent)/(sky input)) multiplier'
   endparameter
   parameter PIXNOISE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.addstars.pixnoise
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'PIXNOISE'
      vpath   'global,prompt'
      association <->global.addstars.PIXNOISE
      prompt  'Extra Poisson noise to add (factored by SKYGAIN)'
   endparameter
endinterface
#
# AUTOMAG.IFL
#
interface AUTOMAG
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A AUTOMAG PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.in
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      helpkey 'IN'
      position 1
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default  !
      prompt  'Input image'
   endparameter
   parameter OUT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.out
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 2
      helpkey 'OUT'
      prompt  'Output ASCII file for listing of results'
   endparameter
   parameter DOFILE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.dofile
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 3
      helpkey 'DOFILE'
      prompt  'Copy results to output ASCII file? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter DOMULT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.domult
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 4
      helpkey 'DOMULT'
      prompt  'Process multiple input images? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter DOCENTRE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.docentre
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 5
      helpkey 'DOCENTRE'
      prompt  'Centre on stars from rough positions? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter DOSECZ
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.dosecz
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 6
      helpkey 'DOSECZ'
      prompt  'Correct for atmospheric extinctions? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter DOFILT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.dofilt
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 7
      helpkey 'DOFILT'
      prompt  'Look for image filter used? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter DOSTDS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.dostds
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 8
      helpkey 'DOSTDS'
      prompt  'Use input table of star RAs/Decs/magns? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter STDS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.stds
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      helpkey 'STDS'
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default  !
      prompt  'Table with star RAs/Decs/magns'
   endparameter
   parameter STDMAST
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.stdmast
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'STDMAST'
      prompt  'Table RAs/Decs/magns override image values? (yes:no)'
   endparameter
   parameter HEADER
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.header
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'HEADER'
      prompt  'Text to write at top of output ASCII file'
   endparameter
   parameter LATITUDE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.latitude
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'LATITUDE'
      prompt  'Latitude of observatory'
   endparameter
   parameter EXPOFF
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.expoff
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'EXPOFF'
      prompt  'Amount to add to all exposure times'
   endparameter
   parameter STARDIA
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.stardia
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'STARDIA'
      prompt  'Diamater of star aperture'
   endparameter
   parameter SKYDIA
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.skydia
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SKYDIA'
      prompt  'Diamater of sky apertures'
   endparameter
   parameter NSKY
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.nsky
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'NSKY'
      prompt  'Number of sky apertures to use'
   endparameter
   parameter THRESH
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.thresh
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'THRESH'
      prompt  'Star detection threshold above sky '
   endparameter
   parameter AVLIM
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.avlim
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'AVLIM'
      prompt  'Sky rejection difference limit'
   endparameter
   parameter BOX
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.box
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'BOX'
      prompt  'Max size of star images'
   endparameter
   parameter OFFSET1
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.offset1
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'OFFSET'
      prompt  'X,Y offset of sky aperture 1 from star'
   endparameter
   parameter OFFSET2
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.offset2
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'OFFSET'
      prompt  'X,Y offset of sky aperture 2 from star'
   endparameter
   parameter OFFSET3
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.offset3
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'OFFSET'
      prompt  'X,Y offset of sky aperture 3 from star'
   endparameter
   parameter OFFSET4
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.offset4
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'OFFSET'
      prompt  'X,Y offset of sky aperture 4 from star'
   endparameter
   parameter DATE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.date
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'DATE'
      prompt  'Date of observations'
   endparameter
   parameter TIME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.time
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'TIME'
      prompt  'Exposure Time'
   endparameter
   parameter GAIN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.gain
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'GAIN'
      prompt  '((Poisson equivalent)/(Pixel values)) factor'
   endparameter
   parameter NOISE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.noise
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'NOISE'
      prompt  'Extra Poisson noise per pixel'
   endparameter
   parameter POSNTYPE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.posntype
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'POSNTYPE'
      prompt  'RA/Dec input as? (degrees:radians:string)'
   endparameter
   parameter RANAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.raname
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'RANAME'
      prompt  'Name of descriptor with RA'
   endparameter
   parameter DECNAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.decname
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'DECNAME'
      prompt  'Name of descriptor with Dec'
   endparameter
   parameter SIDTNAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.sidtname
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SIDTNAME'
      prompt  'Name of descriptor with Sid T'
   endparameter
   parameter SIDTLOC
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.sidtloc
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'SIDTLOC'
      prompt  'Start/end of Sidt cols in SidT decsriptor'
   endparameter
   parameter EXPNAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.expname
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'EXPNAME'
      prompt  'Name of descriptor with exposure time'
   endparameter
   parameter EXPLOC
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.exploc
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'EXPLOC'
      prompt  'Start/end of exp cols in Exp decsriptor'
   endparameter
   parameter OBJNAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.objname
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'OBJNAME'
      prompt  'Name of descriptor with object name'
   endparameter
   parameter OBJLOC
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.objloc
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'OBJLOC'
      prompt  'Start/end of object cols in object decsriptor'
   endparameter
   parameter FILTNAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.filtname
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'FILTNAME'
      prompt  'Name of descriptor with filter'
   endparameter
   parameter FILTLOC
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.filtloc
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'FILTLOC'
      prompt  'Start/end of filter cols in filter decsriptor'
   endparameter
   parameter FNAME1
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.fname1
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'FNAME'
      prompt  'Filter 1 name'
   endparameter
   parameter FNAME2
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.fname2
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'FNAME'
      prompt  'Filter 2 name'
   endparameter
   parameter FNAME3
      vpath   global
      association <-global.automag.fname3
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'FNAME'
      prompt  'Filter 3 name'
   endparameter

      association <-global.automag.fname4

#
# AVERAGE.IFL
#
interface AVERAGE
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A AVERAGE PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN1
      vpath   global
      association <-global.average.in1
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 1
      helpkey 'IN'
      prompt  'Input magnitudes table 1'
   endparameter
   parameter IN2

      association <-global.average.in2
      type    NDF

      prompt  'Input ascii file with a table'
      helpkey 'IN'
   endparameter
   parameter OUT

      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !

interface TBNATIVE
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A TBNATIVE PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN
	type 'NDF'
        position 1
	access READ
	prompt 'Input table'
    	ppath 'current,default'
        default !
 	vpath 'prompt'
        helpkey 'IN'
   endparameter
   parameter OUT
	type 'NDF'
        position 2
	access UPDATE
	prompt 'Output table'
    	ppath 'current,default'
        default !
 	vpath 'prompt'
        helpkey 'OUT'
   endparameter
endinterface

#  TBSHEET.IFL
#
#
#  TBSHEET.IFL
#
interface TBSHEET
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A TBSHEET PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.in
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      position 1
      helpkey 'IN'
      prompt  'Input table'
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
   endparameter
   parameter OUT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.out
      type    NDF
      access  WRITE
      position 2
      helpkey 'OUT'
      prompt 'Output table'
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
   endparameter
   parameter CHNAMES
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.chnames
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 3
      prompt  'Number of characters to show of names'
      helpkey 'CHNAMES'
   endparameter
   parameter COLNUM
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.colnum
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 4
      prompt  'Number of columns to display'
      helpkey 'COLNUM'
   endparameter
   parameter SIZE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.size
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 5
      prompt  'Number of columns and rows to be in table'
      helpkey 'SIZE'
   endparameter
   parameter TITLE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.title
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 6
      prompt  'Title to add to output table'
      helpkey 'TITLE'
   endparameter
   parameter COMMAND
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.command
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 7
      prompt  'Dummy command - use for exit or help. (yes:no)'
      helpkey 'COMMAND'
   endparameter
   parameter MORE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.more
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 8
      prompt  'More help lines out? (yes:no)'
      helpkey 'MORE'
   endparameter
   parameter OK
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.ok
      type    '_LOGICAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 9
      prompt  'Assent to question? (yes:no)'
      helpkey 'OK'
   endparameter
   parameter GTYPE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.gtype
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 10
      helpkey 'GTYPE'
      prompt  'GKS name of plot device ?'
   endparameter
   parameter LINECOL
      vpath   global
      association <-global.linecol
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      helpkey 'LINECOL'
      prompt  'Colour of plot lines? (black:white)'
   endparameter
   parameter NUMCOLS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.numcols

      ppath   'dynamic'
      prompt  'Range of columns to delete'
      helpkey 'NUMCOLS'
   endparameter
   parameter NUMROWS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.numrows

      ppath   'dynamic'
      prompt  'Range of rows to delete'
      helpkey 'NUMROWS'
   endparameter
   parameter LIMITS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.limits
      type    '_REAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      prompt  'Limits of values for weeding'
      helpkey 'LIMITS'
   endparameter
   parameter WEEDOPT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.weedopt
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      prompt  'Action if within these limits? (accept:reject)'
      helpkey 'WEEDOPT'
   endparameter
   parameter NAME
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsheet.name

      ppath   'dynamic'
      prompt  'Name to insert for this row'
      helpkey 'NAME'

   parameter HEADER

      helpkey 'MONO'

#
#  TBSORT.IFL
#
interface TBSORT
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A TBSORT PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsort.in
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 1
      helpkey 'IN'
      prompt  'Input table'
   endparameter
   parameter OUT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsort.out
      type    NDF
      access  WRITE
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 2
      helpkey 'OUT'
      prompt  'Output table'
   endparameter
   parameter OPTION
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsort.option
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 3
      helpkey 'OPTION'
      prompt  'Sort up or down? (ascending:descending)'
   endparameter
   parameter NUMCOL
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsort.numcol
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 4
      helpkey 'NUMCOL'
      prompt  'Number of column to sort on'
   endparameter
   parameter TITLE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbsort.title
      type    'LITERAL'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 5
      helpkey 'TITLE'
      prompt  'Title to add to output table'
   endparameter
endinterface

# TBSTAT.IFL
#
interface TBSTAT
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A TBSTAT PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN1
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbstat.in1
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 1
      helpkey 'IN1'
      prompt  'Input table 1'
   endparameter
   parameter IN2
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbstat.in2
      type    NDF
      access  READ
      ppath   'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 2
      helpkey 'IN2'
      prompt  'Input table 2 (optional)'
   endparameter
   parameter NCOL1
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbstat.ncol1
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 3
      helpkey 'NCOL1'
      prompt  'Column in table 1 to examine'
   endparameter
   parameter NCOL2
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbstat.ncol2
      type    '_INTEGER'
      ppath   'dynamic'
      position 4
      helpkey 'NCOL2'
      prompt  'Column in table 2 to examine'
   endparameter
endinterface
#!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
#  TBTRAN_AUTO.IFL
#
#
interface TBTRAN_AUTO
   helplib   '$STARMAN_HELP_A TBTRAN_AUTO PARAMETERS'
   parameter IN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.in
      type NDF
      access READ
      ppath 'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 1
      prompt 'Input table'
      helpkey 'IN'
   endparameter
   parameter OUT
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.out
      type NDF
      access WRITE
      ppath 'dynamic,default'
      default !
      position 2
      prompt 'Master table'
      helpkey 'OUT'
   endparameter
   parameter MASTER
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.master
      type NDF
      access READ
      default !
      ppath 'dynamic,default'
      position 3
      prompt 'Master table'
      helpkey 'MASTER'
   endparameter
   parameter TOL
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.tol
      type _REAL
      ppath dynamic
      position 4
      prompt 'Triangle match tolerance'
      helpkey 'TOL'
   endparameter
   parameter FTOL
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.ftol
      type _REAL
      ppath dynamic
      position 5
      prompt 'Fit alignment tolerance'
      helpkey 'FTOL'
   endparameter
   parameter NTRI
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.ntri
      type _INTEGER
      ppath dynamic
      position 6
      prompt 'No of similar triangles for a match'
      helpkey 'NTRI'
   endparameter
   parameter TOTNTRI
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.totntri
      type _INTEGER
      ppath dynamic
      position 7
      prompt 'No of matched triangles in all'
      helpkey 'TOTNTRI'
   endparameter
   parameter MAGS_MAS
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.mags_mas
      type LITERAL
      ppath dynamic
      position 8
      prompt 'Master table type (mags:heights:none)?'
      helpkey 'MAGS_MAS'
   endparameter
   parameter MAGS_IN
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.mags_in
      type LITERAL
      ppath dynamic
      position 9
      prompt 'Input table type (mags:heights:none)?'
      helpkey 'MAGS_IN'
    endparameter
    parameter TYPE
      vpath   global
      association <-global.tbtran_auto.type
      type LITERAL
      ppath dynamic
      prompt 'Full fit or XY shift (full:xyshift)?'
      helpkey 'TYPE'
   endparameter
   parameter TITLE
